remarks:
remarks:        You may use BGP Standard or Large Communities to
remarks:        control route redistribution via the route servers:
remarks:
remarks:        (42476:42476), (42476:1:0): Redistribute to all route server peers (default)
remarks:        (42476:<peer ASN>), (42476:1:<peer ASN>): Redistribute to <peer ASN>
remarks:        (0:<peer ASN>), (42476:0:<peer ASN>): Do not redistribute to <peer ASN>
remarks:        (0:42476), (42476:0:0): Do not redistribute
remarks:
remarks:        If <peer ASN> uses a 16b ASN, you may use BGP Standard or Large Communities
remarks:        If <peer ASN> uses a 32b ASN, you have to use BGP Large Communities
remarks:
remarks:        There are additional communities for controlling announcements:
remarks:
remarks:        65535:0 GRACEFUL_SHUTDOWN
remarks:        65535:666 BLACKHOLE

remarks:        42476:65282 NO-ADVERTISE
